  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_fe3c6c38-edef-4a45-8540-7aa23ef646e7'
      });
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer18387985995347799309"> 
  <strong>Falling in love was out of the question ... until it was the answer. </strong>
  <br/>
 <p><br/>There is nothing Aeris St. Cloud wants more than to win her father's love and the acceptance of her family unit by joining the Military Academy at New Hope. But after she is captured by the fearsome space pirate, Captain Chainsword, Aerie is certain falling in love with her nation's arch enemy is</p></span>
  <span id="freeText18387985995347799309" style="display:none"> 
  <strong>Falling in love was out of the question ... until it was the answer. </strong>
  <br />
 <p><br />There is nothing Aeris St. Cloud wants more than to win her father's love and the acceptance of her family unit by joining the Military Academy at New Hope. But after she is captured by the fearsome space pirate, Captain Chainsword, Aerie is certain falling in love with her nation's arch enemy is the last possible way to earn their coveted esteem. <br /><br />Driven by vengeance, Exton Shepherd never set out to save anyone. As he circles the war-torn world in his pirated starship, the Perdition, he only sees his father's ghost lurking around every corner and the looming darkness on the horizon. When Aerie unexpectedly tumbles into his life, he finds he cannot trust her, anymore than he can ignore her. But just like the raging war down on Earth, it's tempting to think he can ... <br /><br />When the war ascends to the heights of the Perdition, Aerie's loyalty, and Exton's heart, are put to the test. But will love be enough to save them -- and others -- from certain destruction?<br /><br /><strong>FROM THE AUTHOR: </strong><br /></p><p><strong><br /></strong><em>The Heights of Perdition</em> is the first book in the Divine Space Pirates trilogy, a futuristic romance series where family, faith, and freedom all take center stage. With religious and political themes, this is one book sure to entertain your mind as much as it stimulates your heart. Look for Book 2, <em>The Breadth of Creation</em>, as the story - and the war - continues on!<br /></p><p>
  <br />
</p><p>
  <strong>FROM THE BOOK: </strong>
</p><p>
  <strong></strong>
  <em>
    <br />
  </em>
</p><p>
  <em>“Tell me your name. It’s a good place to start, don’t you think?”</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“I’ll never give you any information. How could I, knowing what I know about you?”</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“Perhaps there’s more to me than you realize.”</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“You’re a hateful monster! What else do I possibly need to know?”</em>
</p><p>
  <em>Aerie regretted her outburst less than a second later. The captain immediately left his chair and came close to her. Instinctively, she pulled back, but the pad behind her did not allow her to go far.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>As he drew near, she got a good look at his face; though no longer adorned with the pirate’s wig and beard, she could see he was still masked. The apathy, the cynicism, the playful whimsy—all of it hid a deep crevice of pain inside of him.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>The sudden urge to reach out and touch him shot through her. It was quickly followed by alarm and self-disgust.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“From your comments, I would assume you have yet to learn a great many things,” he told her, his voice sharp.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“What do you mean by that?” she asked, boldly meeting his gaze.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“First, your name is no small matter," he said. "Destinies can be made and shaped by your name, though whether good or bad, it is up to you."</em>
</p><p>
  <em>He turned away from her abruptly and began pacing by her bed. Aerie listened to his steps resonate with certainty and distinctness, like a military cadence, as she tried to breathe properly.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“Second,” he continued, glancing at her from over his shoulder, “Despite what you might think, I am not a monster; merely a man.”</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“I hardly see the difference,” she retorted, still rattled by his presence.</em>
</p><p>
  <em>“I would expect that, given your education with the URS. Over the past decade, your beloved Daddy Dictator has managed to ensure your education, rigorous as it is, consists of really only following instructions, repeating the lies they prefer to the truth, and ignoring any logic that would unravel them or undermine their authority.”</em>
</p><em>
  <strong></strong>
</em><p>
  <br />
</p><p>
  <strong>WHAT REVIEWERS ARE SAYING: </strong>
</p><p>5 STARS!<strong> ~ Reader's Favorite Review </strong><br /></p><p><strong></strong>Questions raised about government, religion, and human nature were peppered throughout the narrative, elevating The Heights of Perdition from a mere space fantasy to something much more thought-provoking. <strong>~ Author Jess Jesinghaus </strong><br /></p><p>
  <strong>4th Place in Best RF Christian Sci-Fi &amp; Fantasy for 2018</strong>
  <br />
</p></span>

<div id="review_2535742473" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2535742473" />
    <a title="Sherry Fundin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9198006-sherry-fundin"><img alt="Sherry Fundin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1347125420p2/9198006.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2535742473?book_show_action=true">Nov 01, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sherry Fundin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sherry Fundin" href="/user/show/9198006-sherry-fundin">Sherry Fundin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9198006-sherry-fundin?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9198006-sherry-fundin?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9198006-sherry-fundin?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9198006-sherry-fundin?shelf=science-fiction">science-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9198006-sherry-fundin?shelf=apocalyptic">apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9198006-sherry-fundin?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2535742473" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12491146643547254065">C S Johnson has created a world that was destroyed by a nuclear holocaust and it is easy to picture the devastation and the struggle of the people to survive.<br/><br/>The Heights of Perdition takes us from the Earth to Outer Space and back again.<br/><br/>It was easy to figure out where the story was going but I thoroughly enjoyed the journey.<br/><br/>The people of New Hope, which is formerly New York City, live underground. That alone is enough to creep me out. Above ground is desolate and barren. I do love that C S has s</span>
  <span id="freeText12491146643547254065" style="display:none">C S Johnson has created a world that was destroyed by a nuclear holocaust and it is easy to picture the devastation and the struggle of the people to survive.<br /><br />The Heights of Perdition takes us from the Earth to Outer Space and back again.<br /><br />It was easy to figure out where the story was going but I thoroughly enjoyed the journey.<br /><br />The people of New Hope, which is formerly New York City, live underground. That alone is enough to creep me out. Above ground is desolate and barren. I do love that C S has saved one giant tree and Aeris sneaks out to spend time in it. She has an independent streak, so when it comes time for her to graduate and join the Military Academy, her lifelong dream, her father nixes that idea. She is crushed, but I too, think she is better suited doing something else. She has a green thumb and they are in dire need of someone with her skills.<br /><br />I can’t imagine the life of the people Serious. No laughs. No fun. The leaders say jump, the people say, how hi. No free thinking allowed.<br /><br />Exton Shepherd hijacked the Perdition because he felt he had no choice. It was his father’s invention and he was not about to let anyone misuse it. Him and his crew lived on the spaceship, but they still had to return to Earth for water. Their lives are full of all the things that make us human. All the emotions that entails. And they are allowed to show them.<br /><br />When the two come together, we know what’s going to happen. But, for me, that’s okay. Just because I know how the story goes, doesn’t mean I can’t enjoy it. And I did.<br /><br />All the things that make us human are exposed, the good and bad, the misuse of power, the demand to be obeyed, greed, and love and laughter.<br /><br />The Heights of Perdition by C S Johnson is thought provoking and frightening. What would the world be like after nuclear war? C S Johnson gives us a glimpse of some possibilities. I would love to read more.<br /><br />The only thing I hated was the cliffhanger…but the trilogy is complete and even comes in a boxed set. So…grab your copy now if you love science fiction or world ending stories.<br /><br />I voluntarily reviewed a free copy of The Heights of Perdition by C S Johnson.<br /><br />See more at <a href="http://www.fundinmental.com" rel="nofollow noopener">fundinmental</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12491146643547254065" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer5771479137851782839"><b>*3 SCI-FI STARS*</b><br/><br/>This was an okay read.<br/>The concept of a dystopian with space pirates had me intrigued, but he characters were a bit black and white, and the religion part didn't really fit into the rest of the story for me (might be more explained in the next books though).<br/>However, the story itself was pretty captivating and well thought out, yet a bit predictable at times.<br/><br/>That cliffhanger though!   <span id="freeText5771479137851782839" style="display:none"><b>*3 SCI-FI STARS*</b><br /><br />This was an okay read.<br />The concept of a dystopian with space pirates had me intrigued, but he characters were a bit black and white, and the religion part didn't really fit into the rest of the story for me (might be more explained in the next books though).<br />However, the story itself was pretty captivating and well thought out, yet a bit predictable at times.<br /><br />That cliffhanger though!   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2064950276" />
    <a title="Jessica Jesinghaus" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58113698-jessica-jesinghaus"><img alt="Jessica Jesinghaus" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1471201023p2/58113698.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2064950276?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica Jesinghaus" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica Jesinghaus" href="/user/show/58113698-jessica-jesinghaus">Jessica Jesinghaus</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32510608-the-heights-of-perdition">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58113698-jessica-jesinghaus?shelf=reviewed-for-readers-favorite">reviewed-for-readers-favorite</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2064950276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1542140138136769360">Check out this review, and many more, on my blog <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://jessjesinghaus.wordpress.com'>https://jessjesinghaus.wordpress.com</a><br/><br/>What might become of our civilization after world-wide nuclear war? How might government and humanity react? What would the fallout be? The Heights of Perdition, by C.S. Johnson gives us a possible glimpse. <br/><br/>Aerie St. Cloud is a dutiful student, if not a tad willful, but is eager to prove to her family unit and her government that she can be a strong member of the State military. Growing up under the strict tutel</span>
  <span id="freeText1542140138136769360" style="display:none">Check out this review, and many more, on my blog <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://jessjesinghaus.wordpress.com">https://jessjesinghaus.wordpress.com</a><br /><br />What might become of our civilization after world-wide nuclear war? How might government and humanity react? What would the fallout be? The Heights of Perdition, by C.S. Johnson gives us a possible glimpse. <br /><br />Aerie St. Cloud is a dutiful student, if not a tad willful, but is eager to prove to her family unit and her government that she can be a strong member of the State military. Growing up under the strict tutelage of the State in the underground capital New Hope, Aerie knows she can never ask the questions that tumble through her head. Instead she must follow orders and become what everyone around her dictates. But when fate finds her inadvertently kidnapped by a notorious space pirate, Exton Shepherd, the opportunity to freely ask her multitude of questions and spread her wings is one she can't give up. Exton, meanwhile, must deal with the unexpected complications presented by the strange young woman and the way she affects his long-quiet heart. <br /><br />The world created by C.S. Johnson is, eerily, one I had no difficulty picturing should nuclear world war occur. Questions raised about government, religion, and human nature were peppered throughout the narrative, elevating The Heights of Perdition from a mere space fantasy to something much more thought-provoking. The inner turmoil experienced by both Aerie and Exton were very understandable, and I particularly enjoyed their verbal sparring episodes. With themes of obedience, duty, revenge, forgiveness, love and redemption running throughout The Heights of Perdition took me on a roller coaster ride and left me eager for the second book in the series. <br /><br />**Reviewed for Readers' Favorite**</span>

<div id="review_2573401706" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2573401706" />
    <a title="Charleyexoh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/40224397-charleyexoh"><img alt="Charleyexoh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1541183411p2/40224397.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2573401706?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Charleyexoh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Charleyexoh" href="/user/show/40224397-charleyexoh">Charleyexoh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/40224397-charleyexoh?shelf=net-galley-tbr-and-read">net-galley-tbr-and-read</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2573401706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14018858788935357655">I would like to thank Booksgosocial for approving this title for me to read.<br/><br/>I love reading Sci-Fi books and sometimes I find it hard where to start when trying to discover a great read on the subject. I saw the cover of this book and read the description and I knew that I would thoroughly enjoy this. I’m very grateful that I had my request accepted and I did love reading this book!<br/><br/>Aerie is the daughter of a cruel General of the URS and they live in New Hope which is a post nuclear apocalyptic Ne</span>
  <span id="freeText14018858788935357655" style="display:none">I would like to thank Booksgosocial for approving this title for me to read.<br /><br />I love reading Sci-Fi books and sometimes I find it hard where to start when trying to discover a great read on the subject. I saw the cover of this book and read the description and I knew that I would thoroughly enjoy this. I’m very grateful that I had my request accepted and I did love reading this book!<br /><br />Aerie is the daughter of a cruel General of the URS and they live in New Hope which is a post nuclear apocalyptic New York, the faction frowns upon anything to do with free will and change, even love is forbidden in this new world. It was hard to imagine just what people were truly like here, what people did besides train at the academy and do their assigned jobs. Even marriage and having children was considered an assigned job! What they did for past times and such was a mystery to me and I found it hard to believe there wasn’t more of an uproar against this lifestyle. Aerie was a breath of fresh air, a girl who was adamant what she wanted to do only for it to come crashing down on her.<br /><br />I was immediately smitten with Moona, having a cat in this story definitely piqued my interest further as I love when main characters have a trusty companion such as an animal that they befriend. I was a little unsure about the origin of the Memory tree, perhaps it was simply an oversight on my part as I read but I found the book to be a little slow at the beginning and filled with information that I wasn’t really sure about. <br /><br />Once Aerie and Moona was taken aboard the Perdition I felt the book really picked up, I loved the conversations between Aerie and Exton and I loved their love story and how it grew. Reading about the origin of the Perdition and how it and it’s crew defected from the URS was interesting to read about.<br /><br />The ending however had such a good plot twist when it came to injecting Aerie with a memory loss serum along with the sudden reappearance of Aerie’s mother which I wasn’t expecting at all. I honestly can’t wait to read the second book and the third for that matter.<br /><br />This was a brilliant Sci-Fi/Dystopian book that I would definitely recommend to people. I gave it four stars due to the slight slow writing at the beginning of the book and the fact I did get a little lost in some places when it came to the history of the two factions. Other than that I found this book very enjoyable, the writing style was on point mostly and the dialogue between characters was beautifully written. I read this book very quickly once it got going and it has left me craving more of this series. I had never heard of the author before but I will definitely be looking in to reading more of her novels.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14018858788935357655" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer2489348592179796145">publisher synopsis: There is nothing Aeris St. Cloud wants more than to win her father's love and the acceptance of her family unit by joining the Military Academy at New Hope. But after she is captured by the fearsome space pirate, Captain Chainsword, Aerie is certain falling in love with her nation's arch enemy is the last possible way to earn their coveted esteem. <br/><br/>Driven by vengeance, Exton Shepherd never set out to save anyone. As he circles the war-torn world in his pirated starship, the Pe</span>
  <span id="freeText2489348592179796145" style="display:none">publisher synopsis: There is nothing Aeris St. Cloud wants more than to win her father's love and the acceptance of her family unit by joining the Military Academy at New Hope. But after she is captured by the fearsome space pirate, Captain Chainsword, Aerie is certain falling in love with her nation's arch enemy is the last possible way to earn their coveted esteem. <br /><br />Driven by vengeance, Exton Shepherd never set out to save anyone. As he circles the war-torn world in his pirated starship, the Perdition, he only sees his father's ghost lurking around every corner and the looming darkness on the horizon. When Aerie unexpectedly tumbles into his life, he finds he cannot trust her, anymore than he can ignore her. But just like the raging war down on Earth, it's tempting to think he can ... <br /><br />When the war ascends to the heights of the Perdition, Aerie's loyalty, and Exton's heart, are put to the test. But will love be enough to save them - and others - from certain destruction?<br /><br /><br />Wonderfully written! This book is about two people that are incomplete and yet when they come together there is a balance. And yet, it is not meant to be. I got to the last page and wanted to yell "no!!". Can't wait for book two.<br /><br />I loved reading this book. I'll be adding it to my favorite shelf as it was one I couldn't put down and I know I will read it again and again. <br /><br />I received an advance reader copy in exchange for a fair review. Thank you to the author, publisher, and NetGalley.</span>

It has something for everyone and the Christian side of it isn't in your face but a thread that is entwined in the story. It took a little time for me to understand what was going on and really get into the story but I think that's a bit normal for the first book in a series. It has something for everyone and the Christian side of it isn't in your face but a thread that is entwined in the story. It took a little time for me to understand what was going on and really get into the story but I think that's a bit normal for the first book in a series. Beware that this book leaves off on a cliffhanger so now I am waiting for the next one to come out. <br /><br />I was given this free review copy audiobook at my request and have voluntarily left this review.</span>

<div id="review_2550660551" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2550660551" />
    <a title="Lillian" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24957390-lillian"><img alt="Lillian" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1573061364p2/24957390.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2550660551?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lillian" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lillian" href="/user/show/24957390-lillian">Lillian</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24957390-lillian?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24957390-lillian?shelf=received-for-review">received-for-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24957390-lillian?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24957390-lillian?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24957390-lillian?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/24957390-lillian?shelf=new-in-2016">new-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2550660551" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18091329716660829772"><i>I received a copy of this book via the author. This does not affect my opinion of the book or the content of this review.</i><br/><br/>Post-nuclear war society. Dictators. Pirates. Revenge. Romance. SPACE!!! Y’all this book is fantastic 😀 <i>The Heights of Perdition</i> by C.S. Johnson is the first book in her The Divine Space Pirates series. It is unputdownable (is that a word?). I could not read it fast enough. If you enjoy dystopias and science fiction, I highly recommend it. <br/><br/><b>Aeris and Captain Chainsword</b><br/>Aeris, or</span>
  <span id="freeText18091329716660829772" style="display:none"><i>I received a copy of this book via the author. This does not affect my opinion of the book or the content of this review.</i><br /><br />Post-nuclear war society. Dictators. Pirates. Revenge. Romance. SPACE!!! Y’all this book is fantastic 😀 <i>The Heights of Perdition</i> by C.S. Johnson is the first book in her The Divine Space Pirates series. It is unputdownable (is that a word?). I could not read it fast enough. If you enjoy dystopias and science fiction, I highly recommend it. <br /><br /><b>Aeris and Captain Chainsword</b><br />Aeris, or Aerie, St. Cloud is a graduating comrade of the State government and daughter to the general (second-in-command). Willful and at times considered disobedient, Aerie wants nothing more than to be a part of the military to show her father and unit (family) that she can do it. However her father disagrees as does the other generals. She is placed in a job and told that she can reapply in a year. Then she’s kidnapped inadvertently by the infamous ghost of Captain Chainsword and her life is turned upside down. I like Aerie. She’s got spunk. Despite learning that her truth isn’t exactly true, Aerie perseveres and honestly thrives. I loved reading her character’s growth. It was believable, raw, and honest. <br /><br />Captain Chainsword isn’t really a ghost. He’s Exton Shepherd, a former comrade of the State who was disillusioned and left. Now he works with the rebels trying to build a better world, but he’s also hell-bent on revenge for his father’s death. I won’t say too much about the why and how as it plays a large role in the plot. I love Exton! He sees himself as damaged and without a heart, but he feels so much for his crew, the people he saves, even the stowaway he took when he was after a tree. It says a lot about his character how he treats Aerie when he first finds her, even knowing she works with his enemy.<br /><br /><b>The Perdition</b><br />The space ship itself needs mentioning 😀 The setting on the Perdition is fantastic. Every detail is laid out by Johnson and I felt like I was there. It kind of reminds me of the Star Ship Enterprise….I know different universe but still. It’s massive with many levels and plays a vital role in this book. <br /><br /><b>My Final Thoughts</b><br />Overall I really enjoyed <i>The Heights of Perdition</i>. Aerie’s plight and her white lie wind up driving the plot. My heart broke for her as she learned about Exton and his crew, his father, and the real mission behind the Perdition. And Exton….he just makes my heart ache. Oh and the cliffhanger?!?! Let’s just say I’m glad that the series is already finished 😉 I highly recommend this series for anyone that enjoys science fiction and dystopias with a touch of romance. </span>
  <a data-text-id="18091329716660829772" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12023347260614042049">The Heights of Perdition is the first book in The Divine Space Pirates Trilogy. The Christian message comes through strong in this romantic science-fiction adventure series. The story is character-driven with well-thought-out dialogue. There's plenty of clean chemistry to keep the romantics happy. I own the book and have read it once and also listened to it on Audible. The narrator Scott Senff does all the male voices and Andrea Senff the female voices. Her different characters are more easily r</span>
  <span id="freeText12023347260614042049" style="display:none">The Heights of Perdition is the first book in The Divine Space Pirates Trilogy. The Christian message comes through strong in this romantic science-fiction adventure series. The story is character-driven with well-thought-out dialogue. There's plenty of clean chemistry to keep the romantics happy. I own the book and have read it once and also listened to it on Audible. The narrator Scott Senff does all the male voices and Andrea Senff the female voices. Her different characters are more easily recognizable than his. Both speak clearly and are easy to listen to. I also heard them narrate the second book and they did a good really good job on that one. There were a few glitches in both, like with part of a sentence being repeated. It has a cliff-hanger ending, so be prepared.<br /></span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2237752593" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6870415603828392646">I read this novel on my Kindle before I had a Goodreads account and was just reminded it of it, coming across a new book by C.S. In this dystopian tale (set in the future), Aerie St. Cloud desperately wants love and affection from her family especially her dad, and as she fights for it, she is kidnapped and taken aboard a purloined ship, Perdition. While on board she falls for the captain, obviously using him to replace her dad.<br/><br/>This was a cool book to read. I'd read more of C.S.</span>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Sarah McConahy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/74783152-sarah-mcconahy"><img alt="Sarah McConahy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512844134p2/74783152.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2339454781?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah McConahy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah McConahy" href="/user/show/74783152-sarah-mcconahy">Sarah McConahy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/32510608-the-heights-of-perdition">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2339454781" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9319086337320488925">I really enjoyed this story from CSJ. Good depth of character from protagonists, antagonists, and various side characters, and it satisfied my standards of sci-fi/dystopian literature. Admittedly, I think my favorite "character" was the Biovid. It held so much future hope for individuals and people as a whole... significant in so many ways! Nicely done, will definitely read the rest in the series!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Caitlyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Caitlyn" href="/user/show/71069597-caitlyn">Caitlyn</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2280341664" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11637526220873747656">I absolutely loved The Heights of Perdition! Aerie and Exton’s storyline and relationship had me hooked from the very start. This book had just the right amount of romance, action and drama which kept me reading into early hours of the morning. The ending left me shocked and excited and very eager to read the next book in the series! Love, love, love it! </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2609134548" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2609134548" />
    <a title="Sarah" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18278087-sarah"><img alt="Sarah" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363054594p2/18278087.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2609134548?book_show_action=true">Feb 06, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sarah" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sarah" href="/user/show/18278087-sarah">Sarah</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18278087-sarah?shelf=giveaways-arc">giveaways-arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2609134548" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1676481867701967771">I received a copy of this book from NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.<br/><br/><b>Actual rating is 4.5, but it deserves the bump up!<br/><br/><u>Thought and Plot</u></b><br/>Kidnapped by space pirates??? World destroyed by nuclear war??? Do tell me more!<br/>Aerie St. Cloud only wants to win her father’s love (her father is a high ranking general). But it’s hard when you don’t get to go a top school. Aerie wants to join the Military Academy at New Hope in hopes that this will help her win the acceptance of her family unit. But h</span>
  <span id="freeText1676481867701967771" style="display:none">I received a copy of this book from NetGalley in exchange for an honest review.<br /><br /><b>Actual rating is 4.5, but it deserves the bump up!<br /><br /><u>Thought and Plot</u></b><br />Kidnapped by space pirates??? World destroyed by nuclear war??? Do tell me more!<br />Aerie St. Cloud only wants to win her father’s love (her father is a high ranking general). But it’s hard when you don’t get to go a top school. Aerie wants to join the Military Academy at New Hope in hopes that this will help her win the acceptance of her family unit. But her father puts the brakes on her dream because he thinks she would be better suited for another life and in New Hope you are not allowed to question.<br /> New Hope is an underground city where New York was originally located. The ground above is now desolate. BUT one tree was saved and Aerie sometimes sneaks out to spend some time with said tree, which I thought was precious. Aerie seems to have a knack for growing things. She is also willful and full of questions. But, again, you don’t ask question in New Hope. You follow the orders you are given. Don’t laugh, don’t smile. Don’t even think about having fun. If the leaders tell you to jump, you jump, and the only question you dare to ask is, how high?<br />But things change drastically for Aerie when she is kidnapped by pirates. By THE pirate, Captain Chainsword, or Exton Shepherd. Exton is the son of the man who made the ship Perdition a reality. But when he learns what is planned for the Perdition, he steals it and started his pirate life. Aboard the stolen ship Perdition people are allowed to laugh, allowed to have fun, allowed to smile, and allowed to ask questions. Mostly importantly (well, to me as a reader), they are allowed to fall in love. Aerie almost immediately starts asking questions. <br />Exton thinks of himself as heartless and damaged, but his actions prove him wrong. He cares for his crew. He’s kind to the people he rescues. Most importantly, he’s kind to Aerie, even though she is the daughter of his enemy. He may be driven by the need for vengeance, but the man has a heart.<br />Exton is the arch enemy of her home and her father, but how can she pass up the opportunity to asks all the questions that fly through her head? Worse, she starts falling for him and him for her. There is no honor in falling in love with your people’s enemy and no respect will be earned for it. But how can she help it when he helps her to grow into something more human than she was ever allowed to be back in New Hope?<br />So while it was obvious from the start these two are going to be love birds, the story really does get going once Aerie is aboard the Perdition. The author weaves in some many elements of human nature. Greed, kindness, love, laughter, oppression…they’re all in there.<br /><br /><b>
  <u>In Conclusion</u>
</b><br />This book is pretty obvious on the romance front, but who the heck cares if you know most of what is going to happen when it’s so well written and you have wonderful characters like Exton and Aerie???<br />I’m going to be honest, I’m probably going to go buy the box set for myself. That should say something right there!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1676481867701967771" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2998335598" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2998335598" />
    <a title="Jessica Belmont" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/32433168-jessica-belmont"><img alt="Jessica Belmont" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559243830p2/32433168.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2998335598?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jessica Belmont" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jessica Belmont" href="/user/show/32433168-jessica-belmont">Jessica Belmont</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2998335598" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18014633976101571453">I love C.S. Johnson novels and am always up to reading another one. The Heights of Perdition is a wonderful mix of Sci-Fi, Romance and Christian genres! That’s one thing I really love about C.S. Johnson’s writing. She is able to excel in multiple genres and it is always fun to see what her next adventure will be.<br/><br/>This world has been destroyed by a nuclear holocaust. I was taken right into this novel. The descriptions were wonderfully vivid and it was easy to be transported into the devastation. I</span>
  <span id="freeText18014633976101571453" style="display:none">I love C.S. Johnson novels and am always up to reading another one. The Heights of Perdition is a wonderful mix of Sci-Fi, Romance and Christian genres! That’s one thing I really love about C.S. Johnson’s writing. She is able to excel in multiple genres and it is always fun to see what her next adventure will be.<br /><br />This world has been destroyed by a nuclear holocaust. I was taken right into this novel. The descriptions were wonderfully vivid and it was easy to be transported into the devastation. I love that we are taken from a devestated Earth to outer space and then back again. This was such an adventure and I read it very quickly!<br /><br />This novel raised some interesting questions about government, religion and human nature. I was expecting a brilliant story, and was given that. But, I was also give a thought-provoking novel about what would happen should nuclear war actually occur. I am really eager for the second book.<br /><br />I highly recommend The Heights of Perdition! It’s more than just a space fantasy and I think many people will enjoy this one!<br /><br />*I received a complimentary copy of this book as part of a blog tour with R&amp;R Book Tours. All opinions are my own.* <br /><br />Find this review and more on my blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.jessicabelmont.wordpress.com">https://www.jessicabelmont.wordpress.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="18014633976101571453" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WonfQ6sdAb7Ue+irjp9+8D7M5yI1qqDJVhOXdO7FwReBs5D0styBW+KBfINomr3cE4FHCdsNUmm6Rrq3pio4jA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('efvNTPjGwbGuSObyu524SYu0Xv6Y8Lj3+JmONOBHNgaiwYL74QdBVJiyctpdmHtlpvn+1XZXSlcUzKP3qKjPnQ==')})
  }

But now I know it isn’t true. I was born to be a pawn in the great game of royal houses, married to someone – anyone – my family deems suitable…  Bel would do anything to spend her days alongside her best friend and childhood sweetheart Shae – training in the art of Vairian combat, hoping to some day live up to the legacy left by the mother she lost as a child.  But when a mysterious and deadly attack on the capital lands Bel’s father unexpectedly on the throne, her life is forever changed. In order to secure her father’s new empire, Bel is forced to travel to the distant land of Anthaeus to marry its recently widowed ruler, Conleith.  For any other young woman the chance to become royalty would be a dream come true, but for Bel, the rigidity of court life is like a prison sentence. And while Conleith is an unexpectedly intriguing – and attractive – puzzle… could she ever love him when it would mean turning her back on her feelings for Shae, her first love and last connection to home?  Then a brutal assassination attempt nearly takes her life, and Bel learns that there’s more on the line than just her happiness. Is it the same faceless enemy who attacked her homeland and, with dangers around every corner, who in the palace can she trust?<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"14645899235014913251\" href=\"#\" Johnson is the award-winning, genre-hopping author of several novels, including young adult sci-fi and fantasy adventures such as the Starlight Chronicles series, the Once Upon a Princess saga, and the Divine Space Pirates trilogy. With a gift for sarcasm and an apologetic heart, she currently lives in Atlanta with her family.
